INTERPOLATION ATTACK ANALYSIS
========================================
Variable plaintext byte position: 3
Random sample count: 60

Test description:
- One plaintext byte is randomly varied over the selected subspace.
- The remaining plaintext bytes and the key remain fixed.
- The cipher is executed and round outputs are collected from rc.
- Each round output byte is treated as an 8-bit function of the selected input byte.
- For each output byte and round, we compute a Lagrange interpolating polynomial over GF(2^8).
- We analyze polynomial degree and coefficient sparsity for each round and byte.
